And with zero network access everything works offline and there are no privacy worries.\r\n\r\nSimple choose your output folder, add your files, choose your output format (and options), then go ahead and convert. \r\n\r\nYou can now also specify output height & width constraints to downsize your encoded images whilst maintaining their original aspect ratios.\r\n\r\nFull supported decoding format list*:\r\n.bmp\r\n.dib\r\n.rle\r\n.gif\r\n.ico\r\n.icon\r\n.cur\r\n.jpeg\r\n.jpe\r\n.jpg\r\n.jfif\r\n.exif\r\n.png\r\n.tiff\r\n.tif\r\n.dng\r\n.wdp\r\n.jxr\r\n.dds\r\n.heic\r\n.heif\r\n.avci\r\n.heics\r\n.heifs\r\n.avcs\r\n.webp\r\n.ARW\r\n.CR2\r\n.CRW\r\n.ERF\r\n.KDC\r\n.MRW\r\n.NEF\r\n.NRW\r\n.ORF\r\n.PEF\r\n.RAF\r\n.RAW\r\n.RW2\r\n.RWL\r\n.SR2\r\n.SRW\r\n.DNG\r\n\r\n (*some formats may only be supported on the most recent Windows 10 Update)\r\n\r\n\r\nCHANGELOG:\r\n\r\nVersion 1.2.0.0\r\n\r\nNew Features:\r\n- Support multiple instances of application\r\n- Allow application to continue converting when application is minimised (if attached to power source or allowed by Windows)\r\n\r\nUpdates:\r\n- Light theme, UI Improvements\r\n- Reduced install size + even faster startup\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\nVersion 1.1.3.0\r\n\r\nBug Fixes:\r\n- FINALLY Fixed startup crash on Windows 10 1709 & 1803 builds (due to missing tooltip API's)\r\n\r\n\r\nVersion 1.1.0.0\r\n\r\nNew Features:\r\n- You can now choose image quality whilst encoding to HEIC/HEIF!\r\n- You can now apply maximum size contraints to resize the output images whilst maintaining the input aspect ratio.\r\n- You can now open the output folder in windows explorer using the options button next to the folder\r\n- You can now drag files from Windows Explorer and other apps into the app to add them to the conversion list.\r\n\r\nUpdates:\r\n- Prevent setting un-writeable system folders as the export folder (like \"This PC\", \"Network\", etc).\r\n- Prevent adding un-readable, online-only files -
